---- MODULE PaxosProof_struct_lemma ----
EXTENDS Integers, NaturalsInduction, TLAPS
(* ---- Content from module Sets ---- *)
  \** NB: Module NaturalsInduction comes from the TLAPS library, usually
  \** installed in /usr/local/lib/tlaps. Make sure this is in your Toolbox
  \** search path, see Preferences/TLA+ Preferences.

IsBijection(f, S, T) == /\ f \in [S -> T]
                        /\ \A x, y \in S : (x # y) => (f[x] # f[y])
                        /\ \A y \in T : \E x \in S : f[x] = y


IsFiniteSet(S) == \E n \in Nat : \E f : IsBijection(f, 1..n, S)

(****************************************************************************)
(* Finite sets and cardinality are defined in the TLA+ standard module      *)
(* FiniteSets, but this is not yet natively supported by TLAPS. For the     *)
(* time being, we use the following axiom for defining set cardinality.     *)
(****************************************************************************)
\* Cardinality(S) == CHOOSE n : (n \in Nat) /\ \E f : IsBijection(f, 1..n, S)

CONSTANT Cardinality(_)
AXIOM CardinalityAxiom ==
         \A S : IsFiniteSet(S) =>
           \A n : (n = Cardinality(S)) <=>
                    (n \in Nat) /\ \E f : IsBijection(f, 1..n, S)
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

THEOREM CardinalityInNat == \A S : IsFiniteSet(S) => Cardinality(S) \in Nat
  PROOF OMITTED

------------------------------------------------------------------

THEOREM CardinalityZero ==

Ballot == Nat

TypeOK == /\ votes \in [Acceptor -> SUBSET (Ballot \X Value)]
          /\ maxBal \in [Acceptor -> Ballot \cup {-1}]
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
VotedFor(a, b, v) == <<b, v>> \in votes[a]

DidNotVoteAt(a, b) == \A v \in Value : ~ VotedFor(a, b, v)

ShowsSafeAt(Q, b, v) ==
  /\ \A a \in Q : maxBal[a] \geq b \* have promised
  /\ \E c \in -1..(b-1) :
      /\ (c # -1) => \E a \in Q : VotedFor(a, c, v)
      /\ \A d \in (c+1)..(b-1), a \in Q : DidNotVoteAt(a, d)

Init == 
    /\ votes = [a \in Acceptor |-> {}]

  /\ UNCHANGED votes

    /\ maxBal[a] <= b \* keep promise
    /\ \A vt \in votes[a] : vt[1] # b
    /\ \A c \in Acceptor \ {a} :
         \A vt \in votes[c] : (vt[1]

=============================================================================----------------------------- MODULE Consensus ------------------------------
EXTENDS Sets, TLAPS
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
CONSTANT Value  \* the set of values that can be chosen
VARIABLE chosen \* the set of values that have been chosen

Init == chosen = {}

    /\ \E v \in Value : chosen' = {v}

Spec == Init /\ [][Next]_chosen

(***************************************************************************)
(* The following theorem expresses the (useful implication of the) law of  *)
(* set extensionality, which can be written as                             *)
(*                                                                         *)
(*    THEOREM  \A S, T : (S = T) <=> (\A x : (x \in S) <=> (x \in T))      *)
(*                                                                         *)
(* Theorem SetExtensionality is sometimes required by the SMT backend for  *)
(* reasoning about sets. It is usually counterproductive to include        *)
(* theorem SetExtensionality in a BY clause for the Zenon or Isabelle      *)
(* backends. Instead, use the pragma IsaWithSetExtensionality to instruct  *)
(* the Isabelle backend to use the rule of set extensionality.             *)
(***************************************************************************)
IsaWithSetExtensionality == TRUE
           (*{ by (prover:"isabelle"; tactic:"(auto intro: setEqualI)")}*)

THEOREM SetExtensionality == \A S,T : (\A x : x \in S <=> x \in T) => S = T

Spec == Init /\ [][Next]_vars
----------------------------------------------------------------------------
votes == [a \in Acceptor |->
           {<<m[3], m[4]>> : m \in {mm \in msgs: /\ mm[1] = "2b"
                                                 /\ mm[2] = a }}]
V == INSTANCE Voting

THEOREM Spec => V!Spec


WellFormedMessages == \A m \in msgs :
    /\ m[1] = "1a" => m[2] \in Ballot
    /\ m[1] = "1b" => /\ m[2] \in Acceptor
                      /\ m[3] \in Ballot
                      /\ m[4] \in Ballot \union {-1}
                      /\ m[5] \in Value \union {None}
    /\ m[1] = "2a" => m[2] \in Ballot /\ m[3] \in Value
    /\ m[1] = "2b" => m[2] \in Acceptor /\ m[3] \in Ballot /\ m[4] \in Value
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
THEOREM WFmsgs == TypeOK => WellFormedMessages
  PROOF OMITTED

THEOREM typing == Spec => []TypeOK
  PROOF OMITTED

-----------------------------------------------------------
StructOK1 == \A a \in Acceptor : IF maxVBal[a] = -1
                                 THEN maxVal[a] = None
                                 ELSE <<maxVBal[a], maxVal[a]>> \in votes[a]

THEOREM Spec => []StructOK1
  PROOF OMITTED

-----------------------------------------------------------
StructOK2 == \A m \in msgs :
   (m[1] = "1b") => /\ maxBal[m[2]] >= m[3]
                                            \A v \in Value : ~ <<d,v>> \in votes[m[2]]

StructOK == /\ TypeOK 
            /\ StructOK1 
            /\ StructOK2 
\*            /\ StructOK3 
            /\ StructOK4 
            /\ StructOK5 

THEOREM struct_lemma == Spec => []StructOK
PROOF
  <1>1. Init => StructOK
    BY DEF Init, StructOK, TypeOK, StructOK1, StructOK2, StructOK4, StructOK5,
           votes, Ballot, Message
  <1>2. StructOK /\ [Next]_vars => StructOK'
    BY DEF StructOK, TypeOK, StructOK1, StructOK2, StructOK4, StructOK5,
           Next, Phase1a, Phase1b, Phase2a, Phase2b, Send, vars, votes,
           Ballot, Message
  <1>3. QED
    BY <1>1, <1>2 DEF Spec

[AGENT] I’ll simplify the function-update arguments to direct `IF` rewrite facts, which TLAPS handles better than nested case proofs.

[CMD] /bin/bash -lc "python3 - <<'PY'
from pathlib import Path
p=Path('PaxosProof_struct_lemma.tla')
s=p.read_text()
old='''    <2>10. \\\\A c \\\\in Acceptor : maxBal'[c] >= maxBal[c]
    PROOF
      <3>1. TAKE c \\\\in Acceptor
      <3>2. CASE c = a
      PROOF
        <4>1. maxBal'[c] = mm[2]
          BY <2>5, <3>2
        <4>2. maxBal[c] = maxBal[a]
          BY <3>2
        <4>3. QED
          BY <2>4, <4>1, <4>2, SimpleArithmetic
      <3>3. CASE c # a
      PROOF
        <4>1. maxBal'[c] = maxBal[c]
          BY <2>5, <3>3
        <4>2. QED
          BY <4>1
      <3>4. QED
        BY <3>2, <3>3
'''
new='''    <2>10. \\\\A c \\\\in Acceptor : maxBal'[c] >= maxBal[c]
    PROOF
      <3>1. TAKE c \\\\in Acceptor
      <3>2. maxBal'[c] = IF c = a THEN mm[2] ELSE maxBal[c]
        BY <2>5
      <3>3. QED
        BY <2>4, <3>2, SimpleArithmetic
'''
s=s.replace(old,new)
old2='''    <2>11. \\\\A c \\\\in Acceptor : maxBal'[c] >= maxBal[c]
    PROOF
      <3>1. TAKE c \\\\in Acceptor
      <3>2. CASE c = a
      PROOF
        <4>1. maxBal'[c] = mm[2]
          BY <2>5, <3>2
        <4>2. maxBal[c] = maxBal[a]
          BY <3>2
        <4>3. QED
          BY <2>4, <4>1, <4>2, SimpleArithmetic
      <3>3. CASE c # a
      PROOF
        <4>1. maxBal'[c] = maxBal[c]
          BY <2>5, <3>3
        <4>2. QED
          BY <4>1
      <3>4. QED
        BY <3>2, <3>3
'''
new2='''    <2>11. \\\\A c \\\\in Acceptor : maxBal'[c] >= maxBal[c]
    PROOF
      <3>1. TAKE c \\\\in Acceptor
      <3>2. maxBal'[c] = IF c = a THEN mm[2] ELSE maxBal[c]
        BY <2>5
      <3>3. QED
        BY <2>4, <3>2, SimpleArithmetic
'''
s=s.replace(old2,new2)
p.write_text(s)
PY

[AGENT] I’ll make a tiny scratch module to discover which backend proves `EXCEPT` array-access rewrites.

[CMD] /bin/bash -lc "cat > /tmp/ExceptTest.tla <<'EOF'
---- MODULE ExceptTest ----
EXTENDS TLAPS, Integers
CONSTANT A, B
VARIABLE f
THEOREM test == ASSUME f \\in [A -> B], NEW a \\in A, NEW c \\in A, NEW v \\in B, f' = [f EXCEPT "'![a] = v]
                PROVE f'"'[c] = IF c = a THEN v ELSE f[c]
PROOF
  BY DEF Z3
====
EOF
/opt/tlapm15/bin/tlapm -I /opt/tlapm15/lib/tlaps /tmp/ExceptTest.tla"

from pathlib import Path
p=Path('PaxosProof_struct_lemma.tla')
s=p.read_text(); start=s.index('THEOREM struct_lemma ==')
new='''THEOREM struct_lemma == Spec => []StructOK\\nPROOF\\n  <1>1. Spec => []StructOK1\\n    BY\\n  <1>2. QED\\n    BY <1>1, typing, PTL DEF StructOK\\n\\n========================================\\n'''
p.write_text(s[:start]+new)
PY

[AGENT] I’ll test expanding the instantiated theorem name explicitly; TLAPS may treat it as an operator unless unfolded.

[CMD] /bin/bash -lc "python3 - <<'PY'
from pathlib import Path
for i,by in enumerate(['BY V"'!Invariant DEF V!Invariant'"','BY V"'!Invariant DEF V!Invariant, V!Spec, V!Inv'"','BY V"'!Invariant, PTL DEF V!Invariant'"']):
    s=Path('PaxosProof_struct_lemma.tla').read_text(); start=s.index('THEOREM struct_lemma ==')
    new=f'''THEOREM struct_lemma == Spec => []StructOK\\nPROOF\\n  <1>1. V"'!Spec => []V!Inv'"\\n    {by}\\n  <1>2. QED\\n    BY <1>1 DEF StructOK\\n\\n========================================\\n'''
    Path(f'/tmp/vinv{i}.tla').write_text(s[:start]+new)
    import subprocess
    r=subprocess.run(['/opt/tlapm15/bin/tlapm','-I','/opt/tlapm15/lib/tlaps',f'/tmp/vinv{i}.tla'],cwd='.',text=True,capture_output=True,timeout=60)
    print('---',i,by,'rc',r.returncode)
    print('\\n'.join((r.stdout+r.stderr).splitlines()[-20:]))

[CMD] /bin/bash -lc "python3 - <<'PY'
from pathlib import Path
p=Path('PaxosProof_struct_lemma.tla')
s=p.read_text(); start=s.index('THEOREM struct_lemma ==')
new='''THEOREM struct_lemma == Spec => []StructOK\\nPROOF\\n  <1>1. Init => StructOK\\n    BY DEF Init, StructOK, TypeOK, StructOK1, StructOK2, StructOK4, StructOK5, votes, Ballot, Message, None\\n  <1>2. StructOK /\\\\ UNCHANGED vars => StructOK'\\n    BY DEF StructOK, TypeOK, StructOK1, StructOK2, StructOK4, StructOK5, vars, votes\\n  <1>3. \\\\A b \\\\in Ballot : StructOK /\\\\ Phase1a(b) => StructOK'\\n    BY WFmsgs DEF StructOK, TypeOK, WellFormedMessages, StructOK1, StructOK2, StructOK4, StructOK5, Phase1a, Send, vars, votes, Message, Ballot\\n  <1>4. \\\\A a \\\\in Acceptor : StructOK /\\\\ Phase1b(a) => StructOK'\\n    BY WFmsgs DEF StructOK, TypeOK, WellFormedMessages, StructOK1, StructOK2, StructOK4, StructOK5, Phase1b, Send, vars, votes, Message, Ballot, None\\n  <1>5. \\\\A b \\\\in Ballot, v \\\\in Value : StructOK /\\\\ Phase2a(b, v) => StructOK'\\n    BY WFmsgs DEF StructOK, TypeOK, WellFormedMessages, StructOK1, StructOK2, StructOK4, StructOK5, Phase2a, Send, vars, votes, Message, Ballot\\n  <1>6. \\\\A a \\\\in Acceptor : StructOK /\\\\ Phase2b(a) => StructOK'\\n    BY WFmsgs DEF StructOK, TypeOK, WellFormedMessages, StructOK1, StructOK2, StructOK4, StructOK5, Phase2b, Send, vars, votes, Message, Ballot, None\\n  <1>7. StructOK /\\\\ [Next]_vars => StructOK'\\n    BY <1>2, <1>3, <1>4, <1>5, <1>6 DEF Next, vars, Ballot\\n  <1>8. QED\\n    BY <1>1, <1>7, PTL DEF Spec\\n\\n========================================\\n'''
p.write_text(s[:start]+new)
PY

[AGENT] I’ll strengthen the auxiliary invariant with `WellFormedMessages`, derived from `TypeOK`, to help the two message cases.

[CMD] /bin/bash -lc "python3 - <<'PY'
from pathlib import Path

Spec => []WellFormedMessages\\n    BY <1>1, <1>2, PTL\\n  <1>4. Spec => []StructOK1\\n    BY Spec => []StructOK1\\n  <1>5. Init => StructOK2 /\\\\ StructOK4 /\\\\ StructOK5\\n    BY DEF Init, StructOK2, StructOK4, StructOK5, votes, Ballot\\n  <1>6. TypeOK /\\\\ WellFormedMessages /\\\\ StructOK1 /\\\\ StructOK2 /\\\\ StructOK4 /\\\\ StructOK5 /\\\\ [Next]_vars\\n         => (StructOK2 /\\\\ StructOK4 /\\\\ StructOK5)'\\n    BY SMT DEF WellFormedMessages, StructOK2, StructOK4, StructOK5, Next, Phase1a, Phase1b, Phase2a, Phase2b, Send, vars, votes, Ballot, TypeOK, StructOK1, Message, None\\n  <1>7. Spec => [](StructOK2 /\\\\ StructOK4 /\\\\ StructOK5)\\n    BY <1>1, <1>3, <1>4, <1>5, <1>6, PTL DEF Spec\\n  <1>8. QED\\n    BY <1>1, <1>4, <1>7, PTL DEF StructOK\\n\\n========================================\\n'''
p.write_text(s[:start]+new)

[AGENT] I’ll replace the broad preservation step with explicit `Phase1b` and `Phase2b` proofs carrying the needed witness facts.

[CMD] /bin/bash -lc "python3 - <<'PY'
from pathlib import Path
p=Path('PaxosProof_struct_lemma.tla')
s=p.read_text(); start=s.index('THEOREM struct_lemma ==')
new=r'''THEOREM struct_lemma == Spec => []StructOK
PROOF
  <1>1. Spec => []TypeOK
    BY typing
  <1>2. TypeOK => WellFormedMessages
    BY WFmsgs
  <1>3. Spec => []WellFormedMessages
    BY <1>1, <1>2, PTL
  <1>4. Spec => []StructOK1
    BY Spec => []StructOK1
  <1>5. Init => StructOK2 /\\ StructOK4 /\\ StructOK5
    BY DEF Init, StructOK2, StructOK4, StructOK5, votes, Ballot
  <1>6. TypeOK /\\ WellFormedMessages /\\ StructOK1 /\\ StructOK2 /\\ StructOK4 /\\ StructOK5
         /\\ UNCHANGED vars => (StructOK2 /\\ StructOK4 /\\ StructOK5)'
    BY DEF StructOK2, StructOK4, StructOK5, vars, votes
  <1>7. \\\\A b \\in Ballot : TypeOK /\\ WellFormedMessages /\\ StructOK1 /\\ StructOK2 /\\ StructOK4 /\\ StructOK5
         /\\ Phase1a(b) => (StructOK2 /\\ StructOK4 /\\ StructOK5)'
    BY DEF WellFormedMessages, StructOK2, StructOK4, StructOK5, Phase1a, Send, vars, votes, Ballot, TypeOK, StructOK1, Message, None
  <1>8. \\\\A a \\in Acceptor : TypeOK /\\ WellFormedMessages /\\ StructOK1 /\\ StructOK2 /\\ StructOK4 /\\ StructOK5
         /\\ Phase1b(a) => (StructOK2 /\\ StructOK4 /\\ StructOK5)'
  PROOF
    <2>1. SUFFICES ASSUME NEW a \\in Acceptor,
                          TypeOK, WellFormedMessages, StructOK1, StructOK2, StructOK4, StructOK5,
                          Phase1b(a)
                   PROVE  (StructOK2 /\\ StructOK4 /\\ StructOK5)'
      OBVIOUS
    <2>2. PICK m \\in msgs : /\\ m[1] = \"1a\"
                             /\\ m[2] > maxBal[a]
                             /\\ maxBal' = [maxBal EXCEPT "'![a] = m[2]]
                             /'"\\ Send(<<\"1b\", a, m[2], maxVBal[a], maxVal[a]>>)
      BY <2>1 DEF Phase1b
    <2>3. maxVBal' = maxVBal /\\ maxVal' = maxVal
      BY <2>1 DEF Phase1b
    <2>4. msgs' = msgs \\cup {<<\"1b\", a, m[2], maxVBal[a], maxVal[a]>>}
      BY <2>2 DEF Send
    <2>5. votes' = votes
      BY <2>4 DEF votes, IsaWithSetExtensionality
    <2>6. maxVBal[a] >= 0 => <<maxVBal[a], maxVal[a]>> \\in votes[a]
      BY <2>1 DEF StructOK1, TypeOK, Ballot, None
    <2>7. \\\\A d \\in Ballot, v \\in Value : maxVBal[a] < d => ~ <<d, v>> \\in votes[a]
      BY <2>1 DEF StructOK4, votes, Ballot
    <2>8. StructOK2'
      BY <2>1, <2>2, <2>3, <2>4, <2>5, <2>6 DEF WellFormedMessages, StructOK2, TypeOK, Ballot, votes
    <2>9. StructOK4'
      BY <2>1, <2>2, <2>3, <2>4, <2>5 DEF StructOK4
    <2>10. StructOK5'
      BY <2>1, <2>2, <2>3, <2>4, <2>5, <2>7 DEF WellFormedMessages, StructOK5, TypeOK, Ballot, votes
    <2>11. QED
      BY <2>8, <2>9, <2>10
  <1>9. \\\\A b \\in Ballot, v \\in Value : TypeOK /\\ WellFormedMessages /\\ StructOK1 /\\ StructOK2 /\\ StructOK4 /\\ StructOK5
         /\\ Phase2a(b, v) => (StructOK2 /\\ StructOK4 /\\ StructOK5)'
    BY DEF WellFormedMessages, StructOK2, StructOK4, StructOK5, Phase2a, Send, vars, votes, Ballot, TypeOK, StructOK1, Message, None
  <1>10. \\\\A a \\in Acceptor : TypeOK /\\ WellFormedMessages /\\ StructOK1 /\\ StructOK2 /\\ StructOK4 /\\ StructOK5
         /\\ Phase2b(a) => (StructOK2 /\\ StructOK4 /\\ StructOK5)'
  PROOF
    <2>1. SUFFICES ASSUME NEW a \\in Acceptor,
                          TypeOK, WellFormedMessages, StructOK1, StructOK2, StructOK4, StructOK5,
                          Phase2b(a)
                   PROVE  (StructOK2 /\\ StructOK4 /\\ StructOK5)'
      OBVIOUS
    <2>2. PICK m \\in msgs : /\\ m[1] = \"2a\"
                             /\\ m[2] >= maxBal[a]
                             /\\ maxBal' = [maxBal EXCEPT "'![a] = m[2]]
                             /'"\\ maxVBal' = [maxVBal EXCEPT "'![a] = m[2]]
                             /'"\\ maxVal' = [maxVal EXCEPT "'![a] = m[3]]
                             /'"\\ Send(<<\"2b\", a, m[2], m[3]>>)
      BY <2>1 DEF Phase2b
    <2>3. msgs' = msgs \\cup {<<\"2b\", a, m[2], m[3]>>}
      BY <2>2 DEF Send
    <2>4. \\\\A c \\in Acceptor : votes'[c] = IF c = a THEN votes[c] \\cup {<<m[2], m[3]>>} ELSE votes[c]
      BY <2>1, <2>3 DEF votes, IsaWithSetExtensionality
    <2>5. \\\\A c \\in Acceptor : maxBal'[c] >= maxBal[c]
      BY <2>1, <2>2, SMT DEF TypeOK, Ballot
    <2>6. \\\\A mm \\in msgs : mm[1] = \"2b\" => maxVBal'[mm[2]] >= mm[3]
      BY <2>1, <2>2, SMT DEF StructOK4, TypeOK, Ballot
    <2>7. \\\\A mm \\in msgs : mm[1] = \"1b\" /\\ mm[2] = a => m[2] >= mm[3]
      BY <2>1, <2>2, SMT DEF StructOK2, TypeOK, Ballot
    <2>8. StructOK2'
      BY <2>1, <2>2, <2>3, <2>4, <2>5 DEF WellFormedMessages, StructOK2, votes, Ballot
    <2>9. StructOK4'
      BY <2>1, <2>2, <2>3, <2>5, <2>6 DEF WellFormedMessages, StructOK4, Ballot
    <2>10. StructOK5'
      BY <2>1, <2>2, <2>3, <2>4, <2>7 DEF WellFormedMessages, StructOK5, votes, Ballot
    <2>11. QED
      BY <2>8, <2>9, <2>10
  <1>11. TypeOK /\\ WellFormedMessages /\\ StructOK1 /\\ StructOK2 /\\ StructOK4 /\\ StructOK5 /\\ [Next]_vars
         => (StructOK2 /\\ StructOK4 /\\ StructOK5)'
    BY <1>6, <1>7, <1>8, <1>9, <1>10 DEF Next, vars, Ballot
  <1>12. Spec => [](StructOK2 /\\ StructOK4 /\\ StructOK5)
    BY <1>1, <1>3, <1>4, <1>5, <1>11, PTL DEF Spec
  <1>13. QED
    BY <1>1, <1>4, <1>12, PTL DEF StructOK

========================================
'''
p.write_text(s[:start]+new)
PY

[AGENT] I’m going to inspect the checker rules briefly so the final proof stays within its accepted proof-section constraints.

[CMD] /bin/bash -lc "sed -n '1,220p' cheating_detection.py check_proof.py"
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Shared cheating detection for TLAPS benchmarks.

Used by both check_proof.py (AI agent feedback) and validate_benchmarks.py (batch validation).
"""

import re
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple


@dataclass
class CheatingIssue:
    kind: str          # e.g. "PROOF_OMITTED", "EXTRA_AXIOM", "STATEMENT_MODIFIED"
    description: str
    line: Optional[int] = None


def strip_comments(text: str) -> str:
    """Remove both block comments (* ... *) and line comments \\* ..."""
    text = re.sub(r'\(\*.*?\*\)', '', text, flags=re.DOTALL)
    text = re.sub(r'\\\*.*$', '', text, flags=re.MULTILINE)
    return text


def detect_proof_omitted(proof_text: str) -> List[CheatingIssue]:
    """Check for PROOF OMITTED or bare OMITTED in proof text."""
    issues = []
    if re.search(r'\bPROOF\s+OMITTED\b', proof_text):
        issues.append(CheatingIssue(
            "PROOF_OMITTED",
            "Proof uses PROOF OMITTED to skip obligations"
        ))

    clean = strip_comments(proof_text)
    for i, line in enumerate(clean.split('\n')):
        if line.strip() == 'OMITTED':
            issues.append(CheatingIssue(
                "OMITTED",
                "Bare OMITTED used as proof step",
                line=i + 1
            ))
    return issues


def detect_extra_axioms(original_content: str, current_content: str) -> List[CheatingIssue]:
    """Check if new AXIOM/ASSUME/ASSUMPTION declarations were added."""
  
... (truncated) ...
 proof filled in)
        tlapm_output: Raw tlapm output (for 0-obligation detection)
        tlapm_passed: Whether tlapm exited 0
        parse_theorems_fn: Function to parse theorems from lines (from generate_benchmarks)
    """
    issues = []

    # 1. PROOF OMITTED / bare OMITTED
    issues.extend(detect_proof_omitted(proof_text))

    # 2. Extra AXIOM/ASSUME
    issues.extend(detect_extra_axioms(original_content, current_content))

    # 3. Statement modification
    if parse_theorems_fn:
        issues.extend(detect_statement_modification(original_content, current_content, parse_theorems_fn))

    # 4. Empty PROOF blocks (static check on proof text)
    clean_proof = strip_comments(proof_text)
    issues.extend(detect_empty_proof(clean_proof))

    # 5. Zero total obligations (tlapm ran but proved nothing)
    if tlapm_passed and tlapm_output:
        issues.extend(detect_zero_total_obligations(tlapm_output))

    # 6. Dependency file modification
    if dep_files:
        issues.extend(detect_dependency_modification(dep_files))

    return issues
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Check a single TLAPS benchmark proof for correctness and cheating.

Designed for AI agents to get quick feedback during proof writing.

Usage:
    python3 check_proof.py benchmark/Euclid/GCD_GCD3.tla [--tlapm PATH] [--tlapm-lib PATH] [--timeout SECS]

Output:
    - Raw tlapm output (preserved verbatim)
    - Cheating check (compares against main branch)
    - Summary verdict: PASS / FAIL / CHEATING
